# AppManagerNG — Roadmap

**Status:** Living document — update on every version bump.  
**Baseline:** v0.1.0, forked from [App Manager](https://github.com/MuntashirAkon/AppManager) @ `3d11bcb` (post-v4.0.5), 2026-04-30.  
**Last updated:** 2026-05-18 — Iter-125 closed the T9 **Android 17 ML-DSA Certificate OID Recognition** row as already implemented: live source already maps Android 17 ML-DSA-65 / ML-DSA-87 OIDs through `Utils.getCertificateSignatureAlgorithmName()`, Package Info and Scanner consume that helper, and the focused `UtilsCertificateAlgorithmTest` now runs green after removing an unrelated JVM-test class-initializer dependency from `Utils`.

**Prior (iter-124, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the Eng-Debt **Android 17 ACCESS_LOCAL_NETWORK + Static-Final Reflection Ban** row: Wireless ADB now declares and preflights Android 17 local-network access before mDNS discovery, the remaining static-final `Resources.mSystem` write is legacy-gated below API 37, and the targetSdk=37 audit batch is documented in [`docs/audits/2026-05-18-android17-targetsdk37-batch.md`](docs/audits/2026-05-18-android17-targetsdk37-batch.md).

**Prior (iter-123, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the Docs **F-Droid 2.0 ROM JSON Pre-Seeding Format** row: distribution docs now include F-Droid 2.0 JSON and legacy XML ROM preseed templates, placement guidance, and validation notes for downstream ROM builders.

**Prior (iter-122, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **InstallerX-Style Biometric Install Gate** row: Privacy settings now expose an optional sensitive-action authentication gate, and install, uninstall, and clear-data UI flows ask for Android screen lock before committing the package/data change.

**Prior (iter-121, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **Language-Selector Per-App Locale** row: App Info now reads and writes Android 13+ per-app locales for the selected package/user through a privileged `ILocaleManager` compat path, with a searchable inline language picker and a System default reset.

**Prior (iter-120, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T7 **Amarok-Hider-Style `pm hide` Toggle** row: App Info now exposes a dedicated Hide/Unhide quick action backed by `PackageManagerCompat.hidePackage()`, while preserving the already-present Hidden status badge and keeping the action separate from saved freeze-method semantics.

**Prior (iter-119, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T8 **Hail-Style Digital-Assistant Launch** row: AppManagerNG now registers a dedicated `android.intent.action.ASSIST` activity that resolves the foreground app from assist extras or recent usage events, then offers Force Stop, Freeze/Unfreeze, and App Details quick actions with a Running Apps fallback.

**Prior (iter-118, 2026-05-18):** Parked the two JADX 1.5.5 viewer-follow-up rows after auditing the live source: NG currently has only the core `jadx-core` smali-to-Java helper, not an embedded JADX GUI / CLI handoff / zoom / FlatLaf surface. The `.apks` input and CJK composite-font requirements remain acceptance criteria for the main T12 JADX viewer work.

**Prior (iter-117, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **Termux SELinux Context Display** row by extending App Info's More Info surface with copyable SELinux policy info, file contexts for the app's data/source paths, and live process contexts read from `/proc/<pid>/attr/current` for running package processes.

**Prior (iter-116, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T11 **Inure-Style Batch APK Installer** row by adding a File Manager multi-selection **Install selected APKs** action for `.apk`, `.apks`, `.apkm`, and `.xapk` files, plus an installer batch mode that consumes the selected content URIs and submits each queue item with default split selections.

**Prior (iter-115, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **KernelSU App Profile Awareness** row by extending the Settings -> Privileges KernelSU probe to show the active `su` profile's UID, GID, supplementary groups, SELinux context, and CapEff, with a warning summary when the current KernelSU profile has reduced AppManagerNG's expected root capabilities.

**Prior (iter-114, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T12 **APKEditor `--smali-comment-level basic`** row for NG's current APK/dex smali decode path: File Manager settings now expose `none` / `basic` / `verbose` comment levels with `basic` as the default, and an opt-in annotation stripper removes common `@Nullable`, `@NotNull`, and `@RequiresApi` blocks from decoded smali.

**Prior (iter-113, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T2 **Android 16 `SDK_INT_FULL` Plumbing Audit** row by adding `AndroidUtils.sdkAtLeast(int major, int minor)` / full-SDK helpers, migrating the current Android-16 scheduled-backup ProgressStyle and JobScheduler-diagnostics gates away from raw `SDK_INT >= 36`, and documenting that older one-major guards remain intentionally unchanged because they have no minor-release behavior split.

**Prior (iter-112, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **KernelSU Sulog & Seccomp Status** row by adding a Settings -> Privileges KernelSU status diagnostic that confirms the active KernelSU root-provider marker, reads AppManagerNG's current seccomp mode via `prctl(PR_GET_SECCOMP)`, tails `/data/adb/ksu/log/sulog` for recent denial-style entries, and offers a KernelSU Manager / KernelSU Next launch action when available.

**Prior (iter-111, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T9 **Magisk `--drop-cap` Opt-In Surface** row by extending the existing Privileges capability diagnostic with Magisk version/version-code capture, bounded `magiskpolicy --live --print-rules` parsing, and UI copy that distinguishes Magisk v30.7+ opt-in capability dropping from older or unknown Magisk builds.

**Prior (iter-110, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T19 **SD-Maid-Style Warn-Before-Volume-Scan** row for the implemented recursive File Manager scan path: searching a storage-volume root now warns before walking the whole tree, estimates time from volume size via `StorageStatsManager` when available, and requires explicit confirmation per current root/query session.

**Prior (iter-109, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T13 **Material Files Checksum Properties Tab** row as already implemented: File Manager properties already expose a Checksums action for arbitrary file paths, backed by `ChecksumsDialogFragment` with CRC32, MD5, SHA-1, SHA-256, SHA-512, SHA3-256, and SHA3-512 output.

**Prior (iter-108, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T13 **File Manager Recursive In-Folder Search** row: File Manager now has a toolbar SearchView, a visible active-search chip with clear affordances, and a debounced recursive name/path filter that surfaces nested matches with their containing folder context.

**Prior (iter-107, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T10 **Install-Date Filter + Filter-Applied Indicator** row: Finder now has an `install_date` option, the main list has a persisted install-date range picker/filter, and both main list/Finder show a persistent active-filter clear chip with counts.

**Prior (iter-106, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T8 **Settings Import/Export Portability** row by extending the existing snapshot bundle into the migration surface: exports now include blocking/freeze rule TSVs, imports merge preferences and rule rows into the current install, and UI copy makes the profiles/tags overwrite boundary explicit.

**Prior (iter-105, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T8 **Per-App Rollback / "Revert All Changes"** row: App Details now exposes a confirmation-gated "Revert AppManager changes" action that builds inverse batch operations from successful per-app operation history entries for freeze, tracker/component toggles, explicit permissions, AppOps, and network policy changes, while flagging non-invertible rows for manual review.

**Prior (iter-104, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T7 **OEM Debloat-Blocker Bypass** row: debloat uninstall confirmations now detect Samsung SmartSuggestions / One UI 8.5, MIUI core, and OPlus uninstall-guarded packages from manufacturer/build signals, default those selections to the existing freeze path, and leave destructive removal as an explicit override.

**Prior (iter-103, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T5 **Hidden-Shizuku Fork Detection** row: Shizuku manager package discovery now prefers the installed owner of `moe.shizuku.manager.permission.API_V23` (with the roadmap's legacy service-permission fallback) before falling back to `moe.shizuku.privileged.api`, so forked/renamed managers feed version checks, auto-start/app-info intents, and clear-data warnings without trusting arbitrary package names.

**Prior (iter-102, 2026-05-18):** Shipped the T8 **Tasker Parameterized Intent API** row: public `am://` operation URIs and Tasker/MacroDroid start-activity intents now parse package/user/component/backup/profile override parameters, require AppManagerNG authentication plus confirmation, and dispatch through the existing batch/profile/installer services.

**Prior (iter-101, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Backup Path Exclusion Patterns** row: backup data tar creation now applies default throwaway-folder globs plus global Settings, one-off backup-dialog, and profile-specific custom globs, while preserving the existing `BACKUP_CACHE` flag semantics.

**Prior (iter-100, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Material Files User-Trust for Self-Signed WebDAV Certs** row as covered by the provider-backed destination architecture: NG delegates WebDAV TLS trust, including user-installed CA handling, to the selected `DocumentsProvider`; native `KeyChain` plumbing remains tied to the later native WebDAV/provider rows.

**Prior (iter-99, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **SMB / WebDAV Network Backup Destination** storage-selection slice: Settings -> Backup/Restore now has a first-class provider-backed Network backup destination action that persists a selected SMB/WebDAV/SFTP/cloud `DocumentsProvider` tree as the active backup volume without replacing the existing `Path`-based backup engine.

**Prior (iter-98, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Export/Import App List** row: the main app list can export the current visible/filtered list through the existing CSV/JSON/XML/Markdown exporter, and JSON imports now select matching installed apps so users can immediately run existing batch operations against a saved list.

**Prior (iter-97, 2026-05-18):** Closed the API-36 slice of the T6 **WorkManager / JobDebugInfo Schedule Diagnostics** row: Settings -> Backup now surfaces WorkManager state/attempt/stop diagnostics plus JobScheduler pending-reason snapshots for scheduled and manual auto-backup work. The API-37-only `JobDebugInfo` stats tail is split into a blocked follow-up until AppManagerNG moves beyond compile SDK 36.

**Prior (iter-96, 2026-05-18):** Parked the T6 **Separated Active/Paused Schedule Lists** row as blocked by multi-schedule support: AppManagerNG currently ships one global Scheduled Auto-Backup preference surface, not a list of independently enabled/paused schedule profiles, so adding active/paused sections now would be decorative dead UI.

**Prior (iter-95, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Backup Progress Notifications** row: scheduled/manual auto-backup runs now update the WorkManager foreground notification with app-count progress, current app stage, ETA when enough runtime is available, and Android 16 `Notification.ProgressStyle` segments/point markers on API 36+ with a `setProgress()` fallback below.

**Prior (iter-94, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Launcher Shortcuts for Backup Schedules** row: Settings -> Backup now has a "Pin backup shortcut" action, AppManagerNG publishes a static launcher shortcut for "Run scheduled backup", and both routes pass through an authenticated no-UI shortcut activity before queuing the existing scheduled-backup manual run.

**Prior (iter-93, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Scheduler Battery Optimization Auto-Fix** row: enabling scheduled auto-backup now checks AppManagerNG's battery-optimization exemption, silently applies the existing privileged `SelfBatteryOptimization` fix when possible, otherwise shows a one-tap Android exemption prompt, and the schedule status row now shows the battery state.

**Prior (iter-92, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T6 **Scheduled Auto-Backup Core** slice: Settings -> Backup now exposes a WorkManager-backed daily schedule with time-of-day, charging, network, run-now, and status/history controls. The worker runs the existing backup engine over installed packages with the current backup flags plus `BACKUP_MULTIPLE`; WorkManager is pinned at 2.10.5 to preserve the API-21 floor.

**Prior (iter-91, 2026-05-18):** Closed the safe T5 **Dhizuku Provider Detection** slice without taking the minSdk decision. NG now detects installed Dhizuku, official owner component, API provider visibility, API permission, and Android version bounds in Settings -> Privileges, Mode Doctor, and onboarding. Full DPM operations remain blocked behind an API-21-preserving integration strategy.

**Prior (iter-90, 2026-05-18):** Closed the T13 **File Manager Compression** implementation tail: File Manager now has explicit "Create ZIP archive" and "Extract archive" actions, progress/cancel dialogs, extraction conflict choices (replace / keep both / skip / stop), zip-slip rejection, focused archive tests, and the unit-test manifest override needed to run app JVM tests against the Shizuku minSdk-23 provider.

**Prior (iter-89, 2026-05-17):** Audited the T13 **File Manager Compression** row and reclassified it as **partial**: browse-into-archive ships via `VirtualFileSystem.mount` and `TarUtils` covers tar formats, but the explicit FM "Create archive from selection" + "Extract archive to folder" actions were missing. Architecture pieces were in place for a future implementer.

**Prior (iter-88, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Parked the T7 **Multi-Mirror Debloat-Defs Fetcher** row as `Blocked`: the prerequisite is operational (a secondary mirror has to actually exist; the project ships only on GitHub today). The source-side hardening — byte-length + SHA-256 + schema validation, single-call host allowlist — is already in place from iter-32 and would fan out trivially when a real mirror is configured.

**Prior (iter-87, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T6 **Rich Backup Result Notifications** row. New `BatchOpsService.getDesiredSuccessString(op, successCount)` parallels the existing `getDesiredErrorString` and returns a per-op success message naming the operation and counting the apps it was applied to. 14 op variants covered; result notification body now reads e.g. "Backed up 47 apps" instead of the generic "successful".

**Prior (iter-86, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T8 **URI / Intent Automation API** row as partially-shipped: iter-22's `SelfUriManager` ships the `am://app/<pkg>?user=<id>` deep-link and iter-39's `AutomationReceiver` ships signature-protected broadcast triggers for FREEZE/UNFREEZE/BACKUP/RESTORE/PROFILE_APPLY/INSTALL. Together they satisfy the original "URI scheme + external operation triggers" ask. URI-direct operation triggers (`am://freeze?pkg=…`) remain a future tail tracked under the Tasker-plugin row.

**Prior (iter-85, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **App-Ops Per-UID Control** row (Issue #1863) as already-implemented: `AppOpsManagerCompat.setMode(op, uid, packageName, mode)` already routes through `setUidMode(op, uid, mode)` for non-MIUI ops on Android M+, which is the per-UID path the row asked for. Every AppOps mutation in NG (App Details toggle, profile editor, batch ops) goes through this single helper, so the UID-mode semantics are universal.

**Prior (iter-84, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T13 **File Hash Display** row as already-implemented: `ChecksumsDialogFragment` already surfaces MD5 / SHA-1 / SHA-256 / SHA-512 / SHA3-256 / SHA3-512 for any file selected in the File Manager, with MD5 and SHA-1 labelled "unreliable" to nudge toward modern algorithms.

**Prior (iter-83, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T12 **Per-Lib 16 KB Page-Alignment Indicator** row as already-implemented: the iter-32 commit `df236b6` shipped both the release-gate `verify-native-page-alignment.py` check AND the per-lib UI indicator in `NativeLibraries.ElfLib.toLocalizedString` (lines 335-338), which emits a localised "16 KB aligned" / "16 KB not aligned" badge per `.so` on the App Details libraries tab.

**Prior (iter-82, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T13 **File MIME Type Recognition** row as already-implemented: `FilePropertiesDialogFragment` already renders `<content-type-name> (<mime-type>)` via `PathContentInfo.getMimeType()`, and `OpenWithDialogFragment` routes intents from the same MIME source. Row verified during iter-82 audit; no code change shipped.

**Prior (iter-81, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **MiUI-Specific AppOps Mapping** row. New `miui/MiuiAppOpsNames` static lookup maps MIUI's extended op-code range (10001-10039) to human-readable display labels (Autostart, Background launch activity, Display while screen locked, Query installed apps, Read clipboard, etc.). Plumbed through `AppOpsManagerCompat.opToName(int)` so every consumer gets the friendly label on MIUI without touching call sites. Pure-JVM coverage at `MiuiAppOpsNamesTest` including a table-size lock that forces a maintainer refresh if MIUI ever extends to 10040+.

**Prior (iter-80, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **Per-App Tracker Statistics Panel** row by extending the existing `buildTrackerCategoryBreakdown` (iter-21-era) to also count unique εxodus vendors and append "N organizations" to the breakdown line when it differs from the component count. Surfaces cases where many SDKs roll up to one company (Google's AdMob + Analytics + Crashlytics + Firebase → 4 components, 1 organization). New `tracker_breakdown_organizations` plural.

**Prior (iter-79, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **AppOps Quick-Toggle in List** row as already-implemented: `AppDetailsPermissionsFragment.getAppOpsView` already binds an inline switch per row, cycles ALLOWED → IGNORED → ERRORED → ALLOWED on tap (no dialog) with a toast of the new mode, and reserves long-press for the full single-choice picker. The Inure quick-toggle model is shipped — chip vs switch is stylistic; the substantive ask of "no dialog for common mode changes" is in place.

**Prior (iter-78, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **App Signing Key Change Alert** row. Parallel to the iter-74 Permission Change Monitor: new `SigningCertSnapshotStore` (separate JSON file), `SigningCertChangeDiff` returning `UNCHANGED` / `ROTATED_ADDITIVE` (V3-style rotation, additive only — quieter tone) / `REPLACED` (any known signer dropped — alarm tone), `SigningCertChangeMonitor` engine that hashes each signer via SHA-256 with colon-separated uppercase hex. `PermissionChangeReceiver` fan-outs to both monitors when either toggle is on. New Settings → Privacy switch (default OFF, primes on first enable). Pure-JVM coverage at `SigningCertChangeDiffTest` and `SigningCertSnapshotStoreTest` including a known-input SHA-256 vector.

**Prior (iter-77, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **Install Source Attribution Detail** row. The three install-source package-name lines (installing / initiating / originating) were already surfaced in `AppInfoFragment.displayInstallerDialog`; iter-77 appended the initiating-package signing-cert SHA-256 (API 28+ `SigningInfo` populated via API 30+ `InstallSourceInfoCompat.getInitiatingPackageSigningInfo()`) so a spoofed installer that wears a real store's label but signs with a different key is detectable inline.

**Prior (iter-76, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed two T9 Permissions-tab rows (**Permission Provider Attribution** and **Permission Policy Flags Display**) as already-implemented during a Permissions-tab audit sweep: `AppDetailsPermissionsFragment` already surfaces the declaring package for custom permissions inline, and the runtime permission-flag list (the actual `getPermissionFlags` bits, which the second row's example bit names belong to) is available via long-press on any permission row through `PermissionCompat.getPermissionFlagsWithString`.

**Prior (iter-75, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T12 **Native Library Sizes in App Details** row as already-implemented: `NativeLibraries.ElfLib.toLocalizedString` and `InvalidLib.toLocalizedString` both already prefix each entry with `Formatter.formatFileSize(context, getSize())`, populated from `NativeLib.parse(path, size, …)`. Row was stale; no code change shipped.

**Prior (iter-74, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **Permission Change Monitor** row. New `permission/monitor` package: atomic JSON-on-disk `PermissionSnapshotStore`, pure-function `PermissionChangeDiff`, engine `PermissionChangeMonitor` that filters via `PermissionInfoCompat.getProtection() == PROTECTION_DANGEROUS` and posts a high-priority notification deep-linking to App Details when an update gains a new dangerous permission. Manifest-declared `PermissionChangeReceiver` listens for `ACTION_PACKAGE_REPLACED`, uses `goAsync()`, gated by a new opt-in switch in Settings → Privacy that primes the store on first enable. Pure-JVM coverage at `PermissionChangeDiffTest` and `PermissionSnapshotStoreTest`.

**Prior (iter-73, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the iter-63 Eng-Debt **InstallerX BackHandler → NavigationBackHandler Audit** row as audit-clean (N/A): InstallerX-Revived's fix replaces Compose-Navigation's `BackHandler`; NG is Views-based and the installer activities finish via `finish()` from button/dialog handlers without overriding `onBackPressed` or registering `OnBackPressedDispatcher` callbacks, so Android's default back-key handling delivers the correct predictive-back animation. No regression equivalent applies.

**Prior (iter-72, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the iter-63 Eng-Debt **biometric AuthenticationResultCallback Call-Site Pre-Flight** row as audit-clean (N/A): NG uses the long-standing `BiometricPrompt.AuthenticationCallback` interface which the alpha05 rename does not touch; the newer `AuthenticationResultCallback` is not referenced anywhere in the source tree.

**Prior (iter-71, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T9 **APK Signing Scheme Display** row as already-implemented: `PackageUtils.appendSigningCertificate` already enumerates v1/v2/v3/v3.1/v4 from `ApkVerifier.Result` and surfaces them on the App Details Signatures tab; row was stale.

**Prior (iter-70, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T6 **Pre-Backup Storage Check** row. New `backup/BackupStorageCheck` estimates required bytes (APK + splits + StorageStats data/cache when granted) and refuses backups via `BackupException` when free space is below the estimate. Pure-function classifier with WARN_LOW_HEADROOM / INSUFFICIENT / OK ladder; unknown inputs treated as OK so unreliable signals never block. Pure-JVM coverage at `BackupStorageCheckTest`.

**Prior (iter-69, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T6 **1-Click Delete Old Backups** row (Issue #387) by adding a "Delete old backups" entry to the 1-Click Ops Maintenance section with four preset policies (keep last 1, keep last 3, older than 30 days, older than 90 days), all backed by a new `BackupRetentionPolicy.pruneWithPolicy(maxCount, maxAgeDays)` one-shot variant of the iter-68 engine.

**Prior (iter-68, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T6 **Backup Retention Policy** row. New `backup/BackupRetentionPolicy` enforces count-per-app and age-in-days caps independently, grouped by `(packageName, userId, backupName)` so user-named snapshots prune separately from the daily auto-backup chain. Runs incrementally after every successful backup (`BackupManager#backup`) and is exposed as an "Apply retention now" Settings → Backup button. Pure-function selector covered by `BackupRetentionPolicyTest` across zero-policy, count-only, age-only, count+age union, multi-bucket, legacy-timestamp, and null-row cases.

**Prior (iter-67, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T5 Eng-Debt **Hide-Shizuku Detection Awareness** row. New `ShizukuBridge.getDisplayVersion(Context)` falls back to the binder-reported API version with a `(hidden)` suffix when the manager package is hidden from `PackageManager` queries (the v13.6.0+ "Hide Shizuku" feature only removes package visibility, not binder reachability). `PrivilegeHealthPreferences` now reads through the new helper so Hide-Shizuku-enabled installs surface a real version label instead of `unknown`.

**Prior (iter-66, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T11 **Export-to-Upstream-AM Compat Profile** row. New `profiles/importers/UpstreamCompatProfileExporter` emits the upstream-AM-compatible subset of NG's profile JSON behind an explicit allowlist of upstream-known keys, refusing NG-only `PROFILE_TYPE_APPS_FILTER` profiles with a typed exception and a user-facing toast. Per-profile popup now has an "Export for upstream App Manager" action that writes `.upstream-am.json` via `CreateDocument`. Pure-JVM coverage at `UpstreamCompatProfileExporterTest` locks down the allowlist enumeration.

**Prior (iter-65, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T8 **Importers: Canta + UAD-NG + Hail** row. New `profiles/importers/ExternalProfileImporter` parses Canta JSON presets, UAD-NG `uad_settings.json` (recursively walks every JSON value to harvest package-name-shaped strings, defensive against schema drift between point releases), and Hail line-oriented tag lists. Content-detects format from the file contents. Hooked into the Profiles screen as a new overflow item; harvested package list lands as a fresh `AppsProfile` and opens the editor. Pure-JVM coverage at `ExternalProfileImporterTest`.

**Prior (iter-64, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Closed the T11 **Snapshot Bundle Export/Import** row. New `snapshot/SnapshotBundle` writes a ZIP of shared-prefs (minus `keystore.xml`), profiles, optional tags, and the op-history audit log as portable JSON, framed by a versioned `manifest.json`. Importer is hardened against path traversal, bounded-size, schema-future-rejected, and append-only on op-history. Wired into Settings → Privacy with `CreateDocument` / `OpenDocument` SAF launchers and a pre-import confirmation dialog. Pure-JVM unit-test coverage at `SnapshotBundleTest`.

**Prior (iter-63, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Pass 40 closed a multi-class **reliability/security/race-condition fix set** in the working tree (file-descriptor leak in `OpenPGPCrypto`, native-allocator UAF race in `StaticDataset`, keystore-write race in `AdbConnectionManager`, shell-injection defense-in-depth in `PackageUtils`, GrantUriUtils malformed-URI crash, `ComponentUtils` rules-import truncation on malformed entry, `FmViewModel` null-cursor NPE, systemic wake-lock leak via new `CpuUtils.acquireWakeLock(...)` helper wired into all four foreground services), updated the **Material Components 1.14.0** Eng-Debt entry from stale-alpha to actionable-stable (corrects [S325] — 1.14.0 has been stable since 2025-05-13 per upstream releases page [S341]), opened the **AGP 9.x migration** Eng-Debt window (AGP 10 late-2026 removes the AGP-9 deprecation opt-outs [S342]), and added eleven follow-up rows under §"Iter-63 Research Additions (2026-05-17 — pass 40)". Code-side audit notes at [`.ai/research/2026-05-17-pass-40/`](.ai/research/2026-05-17-pass-40/).

**Prior (iter-62, 2026-05-17 earlier):** Iter-62 follow-through closed the T5 **Restricted Settings Unlock Walkthrough** row. Settings -> Privileges now has a Restricted Settings unlock row backed by `RestrictedSettingsDiagnostics`: Android 13+ installs are classified from install-source metadata as trusted-store, likely sideloaded, unknown, or review-recommended, with an App info deep-link and long-press-disabled-toggle / Allow restricted settings walkthrough. Mode Doctor now includes the same probe and fix hint. This is deliberately phrased as likely/recommended because Android exposes install-source signals, not a public per-app "restricted settings blocked" bit ([S222]).

**Prior (iter-61, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T7 **Achno Samsung Debloat List Cross-Check** row as audit-clean. The one-time comparison extracted 82 package-like tokens from `Achno/debloat-samsung-ADB-shizuku`, found 76 already covered by the combined local debloat lists, and rejected the six exact misses as typos, non-package activity names, or uncorroborated single-source IDs; no dataset mutation shipped ([S215], [`docs/audits/2026-05-17-achno-samsung-debloat-cross-check.md`](docs/audits/2026-05-17-achno-samsung-debloat-cross-check.md)).

**Prior (iter-60, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Backup-Aware Doze Allowlist Diff Banner** row. The Doze branch of `OsRevertMonitor` now runs a 60-second post-write check, snapshots legacy `device_idle_constants` plus the newer `DeviceConfig device_idle` namespace, and adds a one-line config diff plus OEM/system-app-only/Knox-style policy hint to the Doze revert dialog ([S182], [S339], [S340]).

**Prior (iter-59, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T9 **OS-Revert Detection Banner** row. `OsRevertMonitor` now schedules post-write checks for Doze allowlist changes, freeze/unfreeze, component enabled-state writes, and AppOps mode writes; active `BaseActivity` screens surface an "OS reverted your change - see why" Snackbar with target / operation / expected / current state details ([S182], [S183]).

**Prior (iter-58, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Shizuku Root-Backed Avoidance for Banking Apps** row. Auto mode now skips root-backed Shizuku when local ADB is available, Settings -> Mode of Operation labels root-backed Shizuku and offers a one-tap ADB-mode switch with the banking / Play Integrity side-effect tooltip, and onboarding / Settings -> Privileges / Mode Doctor surface the same warning ([S181]).

**Prior (iter-57, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Shizuku 13.6.0 OEM Allowlist** row. `ShizukuBridge` now combines installed Shizuku Manager version / live API version with `Build.MANUFACTURER`, Pixel 9 model signals, `ro.transsion.version`, and Mediatek platform properties to warn on the known Transsion Android 15, Mediatek, and Pixel 9 / Android 16 QPR1 regression classes. The warning surfaces in onboarding, Settings -> Operating Mode, Settings -> Privileges, and Mode Doctor, and links affected users to the Shizuku 13.5.4 F-Droid archive until upstream ships a fixed build ([S179], [S180], [S338]).

**Prior (iter-56, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T1 **Android Developer Verification — BR/ID/SG/TH Enforcement** row. NG now detects the `developer_verifier` service through a new compat helper, marks App Details verifier status as unknown when Android exposes the service but no stable public per-app preflight verdict, warns before install/session commit (including split-APK chooser flows), and appends `PackageInstaller` developer-verification failure reasons to dialogs/transcripts when Android returns `EXTRA_DEVELOPER_VERIFICATION_FAILURE_REASON`. See [docs/sideload-verification.md](docs/sideload-verification.md) ([S172], [S173], [S309], [S310]).

**Prior (iter-55, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the Eng-Debt **Android 17 16 KB Page-Size Compatibility** row. NG now links its JNI library with 16 KB ELF page-size flags, parses `PT_LOAD.p_align` for every APK native library shown in App Details / scanner output, and blocks reproducible release APKs that contain misaligned or unverifiable `.so` files. The release gate also checks uncompressed native ZIP entries for 16 KB data-offset alignment. See [docs/audits/2026-05-17-android17-16kb-native-page-size.md](docs/audits/2026-05-17-android17-16kb-native-page-size.md) ([S148], [S336], [S337]).

**Prior (iter-54, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T8 **Freeze / Operation Audit Log** row as an existing-op-history completion plus two missing UX links. NG already had a Room-backed `OpHistoryActivity` with filters, risk/reversible chips, export/share, rerun preflight, target opening, rollback guidance, and batch/profile/installer journaling; this pass added the Settings -> Privacy entry point and an explicit per-row "Recovery guidance" action for reversible operations. Automatic inverse replay remains scoped to the separate Per-App Rollback row ([S144], [S145], [S231], [S232]).

**Prior (iter-53, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Shizuku Permission Auto-Revoke Warning** row. Direct App Info clear-data dialogs and the main-list batch clear-data dialog now warn when the target is AppManagerNG, Shizuku Manager, or an installed app that declares `rikka.shizuku.ShizukuProvider`; direct privileged clear-data captures `Shizuku.checkSelfPermission()` before/after and deep-links to Settings -> Mode of operation when AppManagerNG's own grant disappears. Batch/profile clear-data logs the same revocation signal for result review ([S139]).

**Prior (iter-52, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the Eng-Debt **Hidden-API Compatibility Harness** row. The roadmap's old `app/src/main/assets/api/api-versions-*.json` claim was stale, so NG now checks in the missing androidTest baseline at `app/src/androidTest/assets/api/api-versions-appmanagerng-hiddenapi.json`, regenerates it from `hiddenapi/src/main/java` via `scripts/generate-hidden-api-baseline.ps1`, verifies source-file coverage in a JVM test, and adds an instrumented runtime probe that reflects active-SDK hidden classes/members and writes a JSON diff report before failing on required missing APIs ([S137]).

**Prior (iter-51, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T8 **Hail-Style Auto-Freeze QuickSettings Tile** row. Profiles with the `freeze` action enabled can now be selected from the profile-list popup as the Quick Settings freeze profile; the exported `QuickFreezeTileService` declares the platform QS tile permission/action, requires device unlock before running from the lock screen, and starts the existing `ProfileApplierService` in ON/freeze state ([S130], [S334], [S335]).

**Prior (iter-50, 2026-05-17 earlier):** parked the Eng-Debt **Apktool 3.0.2 "Remastered" Migration** row as stale for current source. NG has no `org.apktool` / `brut.apktool` dependency or Apktool 2.x integration to migrate; APK editing today uses ARSCLib, apksig, and Google smali/baksmali. Apktool 3.0.2 remains the target if T12 later adds an Apktool-backed decode/rebuild backend, but adding the library now would only add unused runtime deps and a second smali fork ([S332], [S333]).

**Prior (iter-49, 2026-05-17 earlier):** parked the T6 **JobScheduler Quota Stop-Reason Surfacing** row as a dependency of **Scheduled Auto-Backup** rather than a standalone code item. A fresh source/Gradle sweep still found no `androidx.work`, `WorkManager`, `JobScheduler`, `JobService`, or Schedules-screen implementation in NG; Android's current Android 16 docs still make the stop/pending-reason APIs relevant once the scheduler exists ([S45], [S124], [S125]).

**Prior (iter-48, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Shizuku Trusted-WLAN Auto-Start Awareness** row: Operating Mode and the replayable onboarding Shizuku card now detect Android 13+ + Shizuku Manager 13.6.0+ with a stopped binder and surface a "Configure auto-start in Shizuku" action. The launch intent first tries the roadmap-tracked `moe.shizuku.privileged.api/.AUTO_START` component, then falls back to Shizuku's launcher/app-info surface because the v13.6.0 source manifest does not expose the component in every build ([S121], [S331]).

**Prior (iter-47, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T4 **Mode Self-Test "Doctor"** row: Settings -> Privileges now has an active Mode Doctor report that probes root grant/manager/Sui, Shizuku binder/UserService/permission, ADB toggles/pairing, LocalServer `id -u`, SELinux domain, and ABI state with fix hints.

**Prior (iter-46, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Privileged-Shell Journal + DeathRecipient Replay** row: batch operations now persist intent/executing journal state, mark Shizuku/Sui binder death as interrupted, leave crash/kill entries for reattach, and surface a retry/clear recovery dialog from the main screen.

**Prior (iter-45, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T9 **Privileged Op Audit Log** row: the existing Room-backed operation history was audited as the intended append-only log/viewer/export/retention surface, and new metadata now records normalized exit codes plus the remembered LocalServer bootstrap signature in details and JSON/CSV export.

**Prior (iter-44, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T4 **Support Info Bundle Composer** row: Settings -> Troubleshooting now creates a zero-network `support-info-<device>-<timestamp>.txt` bundle with device/build, privilege-provider, feature-flag, remembered LocalServer bootstrap-signature, and scrubbed logcat-tail context shared through the system chooser.

**Prior (iter-43, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T4 **LocalServer Bootstrap Smoke Test** row: Settings -> Privileges now has a runnable LocalServer bootstrap smoke test that performs the privileged-shell handshake plus `id -u` probe, then shows/copies the same single-line bootstrap signature format on both success and failure paths.

**Prior (iter-42, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T1 **`floss` vs `full` Build Flavors (F-Droid Clean Path)** row: AppManagerNG now has a default `floss` distribution flavor that disables optional third-party/network-report surfaces at compile time while preserving local ADB/localhost networking, plus a `full` flavor for GitHub Releases / Obtainium users who opt into online scan reports and debloat-definition updates.

**Prior (iter-41, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T8 **App Shortcut: Freeze / Force-Stop / Clear Cache Per-App** row: AppManagerNG now publishes dynamic launcher shortcuts for recent installed apps when the active privilege path can freeze, force-stop, or clear cache, and App Details can pin force-stop / clear-cache shortcuts alongside the existing freeze shortcut flow.

**Prior (iter-40, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T11 **APK Share-Target Receiver** row as a stale implementation gap: `PackageInstallerActivity` already accepts shared APK/APKM/XAPK intents, `ApkQueueItem.fromIntent()` turns shared `file:` / `content:` / `package:` URIs into installer queue items, and the installer already surfaces tracker, dependency, checksum, and signature-mismatch context before install.

**Prior (iter-39, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the iter-22/T8 **Broadcast Intent API** row: AppManagerNG now declares a signature-only automation permission and an exported `AutomationReceiver` for `io.github.sysadmindoc.AppManagerNG.action.*` operations, routing package work through `BatchOpsService`, profiles through `ProfileApplierService`, and documenting the contract in `docs/intent-api.md`.

**Prior (iter-38, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T7 **Finder: Relevance-Based Search Scoring** row: Finder now sorts literal package-name, component-name, and tracker-name searches through a Levenshtein-based `FinderRelevanceScorer`, preferring exact/simple/token matches while preserving original scan order for unrelated filter hits.

**Prior (iter-37, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T7 **Filter: Permission Flags** row: `PermissionsOption` now supports grant-state, custom-permission-source, fixed-permission, and raw runtime-permission-flag predicates backed by shared `FilterablePermissionInfo` state.

**Prior (iter-36, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T7 **Finder: Uninstalled App Backups** row: Finder now opts into validated backup-only app rows from AppManagerNG's backup metadata DB for package/user pairs not returned by PackageManager, so filters can match archived uninstalled apps while preserving the visible user/state result line.

**Prior (iter-35, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T7 **Finder: Description-Field Search** row: Finder's existing `bloatware` filter now exposes description predicates over the debloat-list prose, so users can find packages by human purpose text from `debloat.json` rather than only package/app labels.

**Prior (iter-34, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Android 16 Capability Dropping UI** row: Settings -> **Privileges** now includes a "Capability dropping (--drop-cap)" diagnostic that probes the active privileged shell's UID and kernel-reported `CapEff` field, then reports root, dropped, present, unavailable, or unknown states.

**Prior (iter-33, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Privilege Health-Check Screen** row: Settings now exposes a persistent **Privileges** screen that reports configured/inferred mode, working UID, mode self-test result, root manager detection with ZygiskNext/Sui markers, Shizuku binding status + API-version/minimum check, USB/Wireless ADB state, remote server/service state, and AppManagerNG battery-optimization status with the same privileged one-tap auto-fix path used by Troubleshooting.

**Prior (iter-32, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Auto-Update Debloat Definitions** row and duplicate iter-addition row: a default-off Settings → Privacy opt-in now runs a launch-time updater gated by the existing Internet feature flag, fetches a pinned AppManagerNG raw-GitHub manifest, verifies `debloat.json` / `suggestions.json` by byte length + SHA-256, schema-smoke-tests the payloads, caches them in app-private storage, and falls back to bundled assets offline.

**Prior (iter-31, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Cross-User Package State Detection** row and T7 **Finder: Multi-User Scope** row: `ApplicationItem` now keeps enabled/disabled/uninstalled user-id buckets, the main list/user picker surfaces per-user state such as `u0 enabled, u10 disabled`, and Finder loads all selected users with visible user/state metadata per result.

**Prior (iter-30, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed T5's **Auto-fix Battery Optimization (Root/ADB Path)** row: new `SelfBatteryOptimization` centralizes NG's own Doze-exemption state and privileged `DEVICE_POWER` auto-fix, profile routine execution and long-running backup/import/restore batch operations now attempt the root/ADB `deviceidle` whitelist path before work begins, and the Troubleshooting battery entry reuses the same helper.

**Prior (iter-29, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **Installer APK SHA256 Toast** row: `PackageInstallerCompat` now hashes the exact bytes streamed into each install session, carries the digest through the pending-user-action handoff, and `PackageInstallerActivity` shows a checksum dialog before launching Android's system install confirmation prompt.

**Prior (iter-28, 2026-05-17 earlier):** closed the T5 **USB Debugging Prompt in Shizuku Setup** row: Wireless ADB setup now preflights Developer Options' USB-debugging flag, prompts users to enable both USB debugging and Wireless debugging before pairing, and updates Shizuku / Wireless ADB explanatory copy so the Canta-model silent pairing failure path is visible before `adb pair` / `adb connect`.

**Prior (iter-27, 2026-05-17 earlier):** landed the **Shizuku Android-17 runtime warning** (`ShizukuBridge.hasAndroid17CompatibilityRisk(Context)` + onboarding banner that starts Wireless ADB setup), the **Shizuku release-feed watcher CI workflow**, and the **ML-DSA certificate algorithm display-name map** for Android 17 post-quantum APK-signing OIDs. The Shizuku row is now mitigated on NG's side but remains open for Android 17 device verification and a future fixed-version floor from upstream Shizuku.

**Prior (iter-26, 2026-05-17 earlier):** follow-through landed the full **Android 17 targetSdk=37 audit batch** (5 sub-audits, all clean: `usesCleartextTraffic` enforcement, `ACCESS_LOCAL_NETWORK` runtime permission, BAL hardening + `MODE_BACKGROUND_ACTIVITY_START_ALLOWED` migration, ECH default-on, ML-DSA Keystore OID recognition) plus a **Shizuku 13.6.0 Android-17 compatibility audit** (now updated after iter-27 implementation). Engineering Debt Register's targetSdk=37 row is **closed** — NG's path to the platform-stable bump in June 2026 is source-side clear except the 1 deferred iter-20 static-final-reflection finding and the external Shizuku fixed-version verification. Three CI/docs hygiene items also landed: **minSdk-21 cascade analysis**, **Markdown link-checker workflow**, and a **JaCoCo coverage rollout plan**.

**Prior (iter-25, 2026-05-17 earlier):** three commit-ready in-progress fixes (`fix(finder)`: regex predicates no longer Pattern.quote'd into literals; `security(installer)`: install-transcript URI redactor closes userinfo / query / fragment leak; `fix(onboarding)`: root-manager probe captures Application context before background post). Stood up `docs/architecture/` (01-privilege-providers, 02-backup-format, 03-hidden-api-bypass + README), closing T11 "Architecture Documentation" row. External sweep added five iter-25 sources: **Shizuku 13.6.0 Android 17 Beta 3 regression** (issues #1965/#1967 — Application Management page blank; new T5 watch row), **Neo-Backup 8.3.18** (supersedes 8.3.17 at iter-18 [S135]). Android 17 stable confirmed for **June 2026** (Beta 3 platform stability locked 2026-03-26).

**Prior:** 2026-05-16 — Iter-23 "Now" tier fully shipped: NG governance docs (CONTRIBUTING.md, AGENTS.md), `main`-branch CI coverage, release artifact matrix, dependency-scan version reconciliation, ADB CVE patch-level banner, package-visibility dossier, minSdk-21 ceiling ledger, and NG-rebranded issue/PR templates with support-bundle intake.

---

## Guiding Principles

AppManagerNG is a "friendlier front door" to App Manager's engine. Three commitments shape every prioritization call:

1. **Progressive disclosure, not feature removal.** Power-user depth stays; it just doesn't ambush newcomers. The Pro Mode toggle is the primary mechanism.
2. **Upstream as reference, not competitor.** Pull fixes and features from upstream aggressively. Diverge only where UX philosophy demands it.
3. **Rootless first.** Shizuku-based operations are first-class citizens alongside root. The majority of Android users have no root; they shouldn't hit a dead end.

Hard constraints:
- License: **GPL-3.0-or-later** throughout. Every new dependency must be compatible.
- minSdk **21** (Android 5.0). Many modern APIs need compat paths or conditional activation.
- No AI-generated code contributions (inheriting upstream policy; NG will publish its own CONTRIBUTING.md in v0.2.0).

---

## Committed Version Targets

| Version | Theme | Key Deliverables |
|---------|-------|-----------------|
| **v0.2.0** ✅ | Identity | `applicationId` + namespace rename → `io.github.sysadmindoc.AppManagerNG`; new release keystore; GitHub Actions release pipeline; NG-specific CONTRIBUTING.md |
| **v0.3.0** ✅ | UX Refresh | Material 3 dashboard; Pro Mode toggle; edge-to-edge (Android 15/16 compliance); AMOLED/dark/light themes |
| **v0.4.0** ✅ | Permission Inspector | Review and bulk-revoke dangerous runtime permissions across all installed apps; critical-package denylist guard; in-app recovery action for previously revoked system packages |
| **v0.5.0** | Settings & Discovery | Settings reorganization by task; global in-app search; contextual help tooltips; in-app changelog viewer |
| **v0.6.0** | Rootless Power | Shizuku integration; rootless debloat; wireless ADB auto-pairing |

---

## Tier Definitions

| Tier | Meaning |
|------|---------|
| **Now** | Tied to v0.2.0–v0.3.0 or is a critical bug/regression fix |
| **Next** | Target v0.4.0–v0.6.0 horizon; high-value, well-scoped |
| **Later** | Post-v0.6.0; valuable but requires upstream landing or prior work |
| **Under Consideration** | Not rejected — needs architecture decision or external dependency |
| **Rejected** | Explicitly not planned; reasoning provided |

---

## Now

### T1 — Identity & Distribution

Required before any APK reaches real users. Every item here is blocking F-Droid listing.

| Item | Description | Effort |
|------|-------------|--------|
| ~~**applicationId Rename**~~ ✅ v0.2.0 | Change `io.github.muntashirakon.AppManager` → `io.github.sysadmindoc.AppManagerNG`; update all `BuildConfig` references | Low |
| ~~**New Release Keystore**~~ ✅ v0.2.0 | Generate NG-specific signing key; document SHA-256 fingerprint in README for AppVerifier compatibility | Low |
| ~~**GitHub Actions Release Pipeline**~~ ✅ v0.2.0 | `release.yml`: tag push → build → sign → upload APK to GitHub Releases; parallel arm64-v8a / universal ABIs | Medium |
| ~~**Reproducible Builds**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 / hardened 2026-05-16 | Release publishing now runs [`scripts/verify_reproducible_release.sh`](scripts/verify_reproducible_release.sh): two clean signed `:app:assembleRelease` builds from the same tag, SHA-256 comparison, and publish blocked on mismatch. Windows maintainers can run the same contract via [`scripts/verify_reproducible_release.ps1`](scripts/verify_reproducible_release.ps1). Gradle archive tasks use reproducible ordering/timestamps; `server` D8 inputs for `am.jar` / `main.jar` are sorted. The 2026-05-16 hardening pass now compares every generated release APK, writes per-APK checksum sidecars, and uploads the full verified asset set instead of assuming a single universal APK. Details at [docs/distribution/reproducible-builds.md](docs/distribution/reproducible-builds.md). | Medium |
| **IzzyOnDroid Listing** | Submit after rename; IzzyOnDroid is faster than F-Droid proper and the primary privacy-community distribution channel | Low |

Submission to apps.obtainium.imranr.dev is a separate manual PR step (out-of-band).** | Trivial |

Audited 2026-05-02; matches SD Maid SE v1.7.x model ([S112]). No work required. | Trivial |

Comment-tolerant `package:` / `sha256:` record pairs follow the SD Maid SE precedent ([S112]). README "Verifying releases" section links to the URL. | Trivial |

### T2 — Platform Compliance (Android 15/16)

Unaddressed items here will become regressions when targetSdk=36 is enforced on Google Play and will break on Android 16 devices in the field.

| Item | Description | Effort |
|------|-------------|--------|
| ~~**Edge-to-Edge Enforcement**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | Remove `windowOptOutEdgeToEdgeEnforcement` (removed in Android 16 targetSdk=36); handle all window insets across every screen | Medium |
| ~~**Predictive Back (Android 16)**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | `enableOnBackInvokedCallback = true` is now the default for targetSdk=36; audit and migrate all `onBackPressed` / `KEYCODE_BACK` consumers | Medium |
| ~~**Themed App Icons**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | Add monochrome adaptive icon variant (Android 16 auto-applies themed icons; supply the vector to control the output) | Low |
| ~~**16KB Page Size Compliance**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | Recompile all NDK `.so` libraries with `-DANDROID_SUPPORT_FLEXIBLE_PAGE_SIZES=ON` and verify linker 16KB alignment; required for Android 15+ physical devices | Medium |
| ~~**`announceForAccessibility` Migration**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | Replace deprecated `announceForAccessibility` calls (deprecated Android 16) with `ViewCompat.performAccessibilityAction` equivalents | Low |
| ~~**Adaptive Layout for Large Screens — Compliance Audit**~~ ✅ 2026-05-02 | Remove any fixed orientation/aspect ratio restrictions; audit for layout breakage on tablets/foldables. Android 16 ignores `screenOrientation` and resizability restrictions for targetSdk=36 apps on displays ≥600dp ([S44]). **Manifest sweep clean: 0 fixed orientations / 0 resizeable=false / 0 aspect-ratio limits across 43 activities. Density bumps shipped via new `values-w600dp/dimens.xml` overrides (app + libcore/ui).** See [docs/audits/2026-05-02-adaptive-layout.md](docs/audits/2026-05-02-adaptive-layout.md). | Medium |
| ~~**Adaptive Layout — Master/Detail UX Iteration**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Follow-up to the compliance audit above. Main → AppDetails now uses AndroidX Activity Embedding on ≥ 900dp displays, with a dedicated wide-screen placeholder before an app is selected and the existing AppDetailsActivity stack preserved. OneClickOpsActivity separates review, backup, and maintenance surfaces on ≥ 900dp displays while preserving the phone layout. Backup/restore review dialogs now keep summary context beside the package/version list on ≥ 900dp displays. | Medium-High |
| ~~**`elegantTextHeight` Audit**~~ ✅ 2026-05-01 | Audit all layouts for reliance on `elegantTextHeight` attribute — it is ignored for apps targeting API 36. Affects text rendering in Arabic, Thai, Indic scripts ([S44]). **Result: zero source matches; no remediation required.** See [docs/audits/2026-05-01-elegant-text-height.md](docs/audits/2026-05-01-elegant-text-height.md). | Low |
| **WorkManager Quota Testing (Android 16)** ⏸ blocked-by Scheduled Auto-Backup | Backup scheduler (T6) must be tested under Android 16's stricter JobScheduler quota model: quota now applies when app is in top-state or running alongside a foreground service. Use `WorkInfo.getStopReason()` / `JobParameters.getStopReason()` for diagnostics ([S45]). **Pre-flight 2026-05-02: zero WorkManager / androidx.work / JobScheduler references in current source — there is no backup scheduler yet to instrument. Item is parked until ROADMAP T6 'Scheduled Auto-Backup' lands; the diagnostics will be wired in as part of that feature, not as a standalone task.** | Low (after dependency lands) |
| ~~**Android 17 MessageQueue Compatibility**~~ ✅ 2026-05-02 | Android 17 ships a lock-free `MessageQueue` for targetSdk=37 apps ([S55]). NG must audit any direct access to `MessageQueue` private fields (used in some root-shell polling paths); `IllegalReflectiveAccess` will escalate to crashes under this impl. **Audit clean — zero source matches; root-shell IPC uses libsu shell processes, not MessageQueue reflection.** See [docs/audits/2026-05-02-android17-messagequeue.md](docs/audits/2026-05-02-android17-messagequeue.md). Other Android 17 behaviour-change gates remain. | Low |
| ~~**Android 17 Keystore Per-App Key Cap**~~ ✅ 2026-05-02 | Audit clean. NG creates at most **2** `AndroidKeyStore` aliases over its lifetime (`aes_local_protection` on M+, `rsa_wrap_local_protection` on pre-M legacy path), both in `CompatUtil.getAesGcmLocalProtectionKey()` and both `containsAlias`-guarded so they're idempotent. All backup-crypto paths route through a **file-backed BKS keystore** (`am_keystore.bks` via `KeyStoreManager`) which is outside the platform-managed Keystore and therefore outside the 50,000-key cap. Zero `AndroidKeyStore` references in `backup/**` or vendored `libs/**`. See [docs/audits/2026-05-02-android17-keystore-key-cap.md](docs/audits/2026-05-02-android17-keystore-key-cap.md). | Low |

### T3 — Critical Bug Fixes & Security Debt

These are `FIXME` / security issues identified in source that should not wait for a feature release.

| Item | File | Description | Effort |
|------|------|-------------|--------|
| ~~**Keystore Password Security**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | `KeyStoreUtils.java` | Use `char[]` instead of `String` for keystore passwords (String is interned in heap; not clearable) | Low |
| ~~**ABX-to-XML Lossless Fix**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | `CodeEditorViewModel.java` | Current ABX→XML conversion is lossy; update serializer to round-trip without data loss | Medium |
| ~~**Intent Interceptor OPEN_DOCUMENT**~~ ✅ v0.3.0 | `ActivityInterceptor.java` | Interceptor permanently breaks `android.intent.action.OPEN_DOCUMENT` (Issue #1767, 2 reactions); fix dispatch logic | Medium |
| ~~**Utils.java i18n (×5)**~~ ✅ 2026-05-02 | `Utils.java` | Soft-input / service-flag / activity-flag / input-feature flag strings now pull from `strings.xml`; `getProtectionLevelString` keeps Android's canonical manifest-protection-level tokens (`dangerous`, `signature\|privileged`, etc.) intentionally untranslated — they are technical identifiers, and a `protectionLevel.contains("dangerous")` check exists in `AppDetailsPermissionsFragment`. | Low |
| ~~**Android 18 Implicit URI Grant Removal**~~ ✅ 2026-05-02 | `PackageInstaller` / share intents | All seven outgoing `ACTION_SEND` / `ACTION_SEND_MULTIPLE` paths that carry a content URI now set both `FLAG_GRANT_READ_URI_PERMISSION` and an explicit `ClipData` (multi-item for `SEND_MULTIPLE`) so the chooser target receives read access without relying on Android's implicit auto-grant. Three text-only sender paths (no URI) left untouched. Zero `IMAGE_CAPTURE` callers in source. `PackageInstaller` install path streams via `openWrite()` and is unaffected. See [docs/audits/2026-05-02-android18-implicit-uri-grant.md](docs/audits/2026-05-02-android18-implicit-uri-grant.md). | Low |

Wired from `AppManager.onCreate()`. Listener-side wiring to harvest the resulting profile artifacts and attach them to the diagnostic ZIP is deferred until API 37 is on a real device for end-to-end test. | Low |

---

## Next

### T5 — Rootless Users (Shizuku)

Shizuku support is the single most-requested upstream feature with 31 reactions across 5 years ([S02]). It unblocks the majority of AM operations for users without root. Canta ([S19]) and SmartPack Package Manager ([S21]) already ship Shizuku integration; AM/NG without it is at a structural disadvantage for casual users.

| Item | Description | Effort |
|------|-------------|--------|
| ~~**Shizuku Privilege Provider**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Added Shizuku/Sui UserService as a first-class privilege path alongside root and ADB, with automatic runtime detection, permission recovery, mode-selection status, onboarding copy, and Android 7.0+ provider gating. | High |
| ~~**Wireless ADB Auto-Pairing**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Added guided Android 11+ Wireless ADB setup from onboarding, persisted successful pairing metadata, surfaced remembered-device status in onboarding/settings, and kept ADB-over-TCP fallback guidance for older devices. | Medium |
| ~~**Rootless Debloat (Shizuku)**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Added a Shizuku/ADB shell `pm uninstall --user <id>` path for Debloater uninstall batches, bypassing accessibility prompts when the privileged shell is active. Selection confirmation now summarizes android-debloat-list safety ratings, dependency/required-by warnings, and high-risk examples before removal; Debloater rows also surface dependency counts inline. | Medium |
| ~~**Factory-Reset Before System App Uninstall**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Updated uninstall flows to reset updated system apps back to the factory version before user-scope removal, using `pm uninstall-system-updates` when a Shizuku/ADB/root shell is active and surfacing the reset in Debloater confirmation/card copy. | Low |
| ~~**Debloat Presets**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Added Privacy, Gaming, and Minimal OEM Debloater presets that select installed recommendations as curated batches, preview match counts and rationale, then route through the reviewed freeze/remove confirmations before applying the recommended action. | Medium |

| ~~**Install Existing Apps via `package:` URI**~~ ✅ 2026-05-14 | Completed the upstream v4.0.5 model: external `package:package-name` view/install intents now resolve to NG's installer, the existing `PackageInstallerCompat.installExisting()` path reinstalls an already-present APK for the selected/current user, and `SEND_MULTIPLE` intake now combines package/file/content URIs from both `EXTRA_STREAM` and `ClipData` without duplicates. | Low (pull) |

Tap → `PackageManagerCompat.forceStopPackage(packageName, userId)` → `ActivityManagerCompat.getActivityManager().forceStopPackage(...)`. Reference: Hail v1.9.0 / [S65]. | Low |
| ~~**Dhizuku Provider Detection (DeviceOwner path)**~~ ✅ 2026-05-18 | Added a no-dependency `dhizuku/DhizukuBridge` that detects the official `com.rosan.dhizuku/.server.DhizukuDAReceiver` owner component, installed manager version, API provider visibility, API permission state, and Android 8-16 support bounds. ### T6 — Backup Polish

Neo Backup ([S20]) and Titanium Backup are the benchmark. AM's backup engine is competitive; the UX around scheduling, retention, and verification is not.

| Item | Description | Effort |
|------|-------------|--------|
| ~~**Scheduled Auto-Backup Core**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-92) | New `backup/schedule/AutoBackupScheduler` and `AutoBackupWorker` add a WorkManager-backed daily backup schedule with time-of-day, charging-state, and network-availability constraints ([S09]). Settings -> Backup now exposes enable/disable, time picker, require-charging switch, network condition picker, manual "Run scheduled backup now", and a status row with last-run/result history. The worker enumerates installed `UserPackagePair`s, runs the existing backup engine with the user's current backup flags plus `BACKUP_MULTIPLE`, records success/partial/failure results, and posts result notifications. WorkManager is pinned at 2.10.5 and app code compiles against the existing Guava runtime for WorkManager's exposed `ListenableFuture` API so the feature keeps AppManagerNG's API-21 floor. Pure-JVM coverage: [`AutoBackupSchedulerTest`](app/src/test/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/schedule/AutoBackupSchedulerTest.java) covers initial-delay rollover, clamping, and network mapping. | Medium |
| ~~**Backup Retention Policy**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-17 (iter-68) | New `backup/BackupRetentionPolicy` enforces two independent caps: max backups per `(packageName, userId, backupName)` bucket and max age in days. Both default to `0` (unlimited). Pure-function `selectStaleBackups()` groups by bucket so user-named "preinstall" snapshots prune independently from the daily auto-backup chain, sorts newest-first, then applies count and age caps as a union. Wired into `BackupManager#backup` so the policy runs incrementally after every successful backup; also exposed as a "Apply retention now" button in Settings → Backup that calls `pruneAll()`. Backups with `backupTime <= 0` (legacy / unknown) are skipped from age-based pruning so a missing timestamp can't be misread as "infinitely old". Pure-JVM coverage: [`BackupRetentionPolicyTest`](app/src/test/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/BackupRetentionPolicyTest.java) covers zero-policy no-op, count-cap-only, age-cap-only, count+age union, multi-bucket grouping, legacy-timestamp skip, and null-row tolerance. ([S41] model.) | T6 | **Next (shipped)** |
| ~~**1-Click Delete Old Backups**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-17 (iter-69) | Closed by adding a "Delete old backups" entry to the 1-Click Ops Maintenance section. Four preset policies — keep last 1 per app, keep last 3 per app, older-than-30-days, older-than-90-days — all share the existing `BackupRetentionPolicy.pruneWithPolicy(maxCount, maxAgeDays)` engine from iter-68 (new one-shot variant that takes explicit caps without writing to the persistent prefs). Confirmation dialog before each apply. Issue #387 ([S33]). | T6 | **Next (shipped)** |
| ~~**Backup Integrity Verification**~~ ✅ closed 2026-05-16 (already implemented) | [`BackupOp`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/BackupOp.java) computes a SHA-256 digest per backup file via `DigestUtils.getHexDigest(mMetadata.info.checksumAlgo, file)` and persists the table through [`BackupItems.Checksum`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/BackupItems.java#L535). [`RestoreOp`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/RestoreOp.java) re-computes the digest for `info.json`, `meta.json`, master key, data tar parts, certificates, and misc files at restore time and raises `BackupException` on mismatch. The checksum algorithm is stored in metadata so backups created with a future stronger digest can still be restored. | Medium |
| ~~**AES-256 Backup Encryption**~~ ✅ closed 2026-05-16 (already implemented, key derivation differs from spec) | NG ships AES-256-GCM backup encryption via [`AESCrypto`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/crypto/AESCrypto.java) selected through [`CryptoUtils.MODE_AES`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/CryptoUtils.java) in the backup-mode picker. The implementation uses Android Keystore-backed `SecretKey` material (more secure than the original row's PBKDF2 sketch — keys are non-exportable and hardware-isolated where TEE is available) and the recently-shipped metadata-v6 per-file IV derivation. 128-bit GCM MAC since v3.0.3; older 32-bit MAC backups remain restorable. | Medium |
| ~~**PGP Backup Encryption**~~ ✅ closed 2026-05-16 (already implemented) | [`OpenPGPCrypto`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/crypto/OpenPGPCrypto.java) integrates the OpenIntents OpenPGP API; encrypted backups go through any OpenPGP provider the user has installed (OpenKeychain is the canonical option). Provider selection lives at `Prefs.Encryption.getOpenPgpProvider()`. Selected via `CryptoUtils.MODE_OPEN_PGP` alongside AES / RSA / ECC in the backup mode picker. Reference: Neo Backup v8.3.12 ([S41]). | Medium |
| ~~**Backup Sharing Button**~~ ✅ 2026-05-16 | The Restore-Single popup menu now exposes a "Share backup" action (enabled when exactly one backup is selected). Reuses the existing [`SharableItems`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/fm/SharableItems.java) helper to wrap every file under the backup directory in a single `ACTION_SEND_MULTIPLE` chooser intent through `FmProvider`. Encrypted backups stay encrypted on the way out — the recipient still needs the user's AppManagerNG encryption key to restore. Reference: Neo Backup v8.3.17 ([S41]). | Low |
| ~~**Launcher Shortcuts for Backup Schedules**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-94) | Settings -> Backup now has a "Pin backup shortcut" action that requests a pinned launcher shortcut with a stable scheduled-backup ID and `ic_backup_restore` icon. AppManagerNG also exposes a static "Run scheduled backup" launcher shortcut from `res/xml/shortcuts.xml`. Both routes enqueue the same manual scheduled-backup WorkManager request through `AutoBackupShortcutActivity`, which extends `BaseActivity` so app authentication still applies before the operation is queued. Neo Backup v8.3.17 model ([S41]). | Low |
| ~~**Rich Backup Result Notifications**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-17 (iter-87) | New `BatchOpsService.getDesiredSuccessString(op, successCount)` parallel to the existing `getDesiredErrorString` returns a per-op success message that names the operation and counts the apps it was applied to. 14 op variants covered: backup, backup-apk, restore, delete-backup, import-backups, freeze, advanced-freeze (shares freeze plural), unfreeze, force-stop, clear-data, clear-cache, block-trackers, unblock-trackers, uninstall, dexopt — each backed by its own `alert_succeeded_*` plural. Generic "the operation was successful" remains the fallback for ops without a tailored string. Result notification body now reads e.g. "Backed up 47 apps" instead of the generic "successful". Total size aggregation is out-of-scope for the notification fast-path (would require walking `BackupDao` at notification time). SD Maid SE scheduler model ([S42], [S112]). | Low |
| ~~**Backup Progress Notifications**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-95) | `AutoBackupWorker` now passes a Worker-specific `ProgressHandler` into the existing `BatchOpsManager` / `BackupManager` progress path instead of running scheduled backups silently behind a generic foreground notification. The foreground notification shows app-count progress, current app label/stage, and ETA once enough runtime exists; API 36+ builds use platform `Notification.ProgressStyle` segments plus a current-progress point marker, and older devices keep the standard `NotificationCompat#setProgress()` fallback. The existing final success/partial/failure result notification remains unchanged. ([S46]). | Low |
| ~~**Pre-Backup Storage Check**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-17 (iter-70) | New `backup/BackupStorageCheck` evaluates required-vs-available bytes before `BackupManager#backup()` starts the runner. Estimator: base APK + split APKs + (on API 26+, when `PACKAGE_USAGE_STATS` is granted) `StorageStatsManager.queryStatsForPackage()` data + cache; multiplied by `BACKUP_OVERHEAD_FACTOR` 1.2× for tar/metadata/per-file checksums. Free-space query uses `File.getUsableSpace()` on the backup volume. Pure-function `classify(estimated, free, safetyMargin)` ladder: `INSUFFICIENT` (free < estimated, backup refused with `BackupException`) / `WARN_LOW_HEADROOM` (headroom < 64 MB safety margin, backup proceeds) / `OK`. Treats either side being zero or negative as "unknown" → `OK`, so missing `PACKAGE_USAGE_STATS` or SAF-backed volumes never block a backup on unreliable input. Pure-JVM coverage: [`BackupStorageCheckTest`](app/src/test/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/BackupStorageCheckTest.java) covers six cases including the exact-margin boundary and the zero-margin degenerate. Reference: [S41]. | T6 | **Next (shipped)** |
| **Separated Active/Paused Schedule Lists** ⏸ blocked-by multi-schedule profiles | Parked 2026-05-18 (iter-96). The current Scheduled Auto-Backup implementation has one global schedule exposed as Settings -> Backup preferences, not a collection of independently named schedules. There is no flat unsorted schedule list to separate yet. Reopen only after NG adds multiple schedule profiles/tags; at that point, display enabled and disabled backup schedules in distinct active/paused sections. Neo Backup v8.3.15 model ([S41]). | Low |
| ~~**Backup Tag Autocomplete**~~ ✅ 2026-05-08 (closed 2026-05-16 as duplicate) | Already shipped under iter-21 "Neo-Backup-Style Existing-Tag Suggestions": [`BackupFragment.collectExistingBackupNames()`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/backup/dialog/BackupFragment.java) walks every `BackupInfo` in scope, harvests distinct non-empty `BackupMetadataV5.metadata.backupName` values, and feeds the de-duplicated `LinkedHashSet` into `TextInputDropdownDialogBuilder.setDropdownItems()`. The multi-backup name dialog now autocompletes from prior labels. When the planned multi-tag DAO lands, the same `setDropdownItems` adapter pattern can be reused for the tag-add dialog with zero changes. Reference: [S41]. | Low |
| ~~**Scheduler Battery Optimization Auto-Fix**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-93) | When the user enables Scheduled Auto-Backup, Settings -> Backup now checks AppManagerNG's battery-optimization exemption. | ~~**WorkManager / JobDebugInfo Schedule Diagnostics**~~ ✅ API-36 slice shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-97) | Settings -> Backup now includes scheduled-backup diagnostics in the status row: the latest scheduled and manual WorkManager requests show state, run attempt, next run time, and `WorkInfo.getStopReason()`. | **JobDebugInfo Pending Reason Stats (API 37)** ⏸ blocked-by compileSdk 37 | Once AppManagerNG raises compile SDK beyond 36, surface `JobDebugInfo.getPendingJobReasonStats()` in scheduled-backup history or operation logs when available ([S53]). | ~~**Export/Import App List**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-18 (iter-98) | Main-list overflow now exports the current visible/filtered app list through the existing CSV/JSON/XML/Markdown exporter, while selection mode keeps the selected-app export path.
