### Iter-64 Closures (2026-05-17)

| Item | Result |
|------|--------|
| **Snapshot Bundle Export/Import** | Closed the T11 row by adding `snapshot/SnapshotBundle` (ZIP writer/reader with `manifest.json` schema-versioning, op-history JSON serialization for cross-applicationId portability, keystore-prefs exclusion, ZIP traversal/size hardening, and append-only op-history restore), `snapshot/SnapshotImportException`, two new prefs (`snapshot_export` / `snapshot_import`) on Settings → Privacy backed by SAF `CreateDocument` / `OpenDocument` launchers with a pre-import confirmation dialog, and pure-JVM coverage in `SnapshotBundleTest`. |

### Iter-63 Closures (2026-05-17)

Code-side reliability/security pass executed by the autonomous research-run agent. Fixes applied to the working tree (uncommitted at the time of writing this entry); the maintainer is expected to commit as a single `fix(audit): pass-40 reliability/security findings` commit or pick-and-stage individually. Coverage:

| File | Class of fix | Description |
|------|--------------|-------------|
| [`crypto/OpenPGPCrypto.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/crypto/OpenPGPCrypto.java) | FD leak | `doActionForFiles` opened `InputStream`/`OutputStream` per file but `OpenPgpApi#executeApi` never closes its streams — leaked two FDs per encrypt/decrypt iteration. Wrapped in try-with-resources. Also hardened `close()` against double-unregister (`IllegalArgumentException` on duplicate `unregisterReceiver`). |
| [`uri/GrantUriUtils.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/uri/GrantUriUtils.java) | Crash | `getRealPath` called `dirtyFile.substring(0, splitIndex)` where `splitIndex = dirtyFile.indexOf(":", 1)` — a malformed SAF URI without a `:` returned `-1` and crashed the URI-permission display dialog. Added `-1` guard, `Uri.parse` try/catch, and null-authority fallback. |
| [`adb/AdbConnectionManager.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/adb/AdbConnectionManager.java), [`crypto/ks/KeyStoreManager.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/crypto/ks/KeyStoreManager.java), [`db/AppsDb.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/db/AppsDb.java) | Lazy-init race | Three unsynchronized `getInstance()` patterns. Worst case: AdbConnectionManager concurrent first-callers both race in `KeyStoreManager.addKeyPair(ADB_KEY_ALIAS, …, overwrite=true)`. Added `synchronized` modifier on all three. |
| [`StaticDataset.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/StaticDataset.java) | Native UAF race | `getSearchableTrackerSignatures` / `cleanup` mutate a static `AhoCorasick` that owns native memory; race between two first-callers leaked the unreferenced instance, race with `cleanup()` was a use-after-free in JNI. Synchronized all four mutating accessors. |
| [`utils/PackageUtils.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/utils/PackageUtils.java) + [`app/src/test/java/.../PackageUtilsPackageNameValidationTest.java`](app/src/test/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/utils/PackageUtilsPackageNameValidationTest.java) | Shell-injection defense-in-depth | `getHiddenCodePathOrDefault` concatenated `packageName` into a shell-evaluated `pm dump <pkg> \| grep codePath` pipeline. Added `isPlausiblePackageName` (rejects anything outside `[A-Za-z0-9._]`, empty, oversized, digit-leading) and a unit-test locking down shell-metacharacter rejection. |
| [`fm/FmViewModel.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/fm/FmViewModel.java) | Null-cursor NPE | `ContentResolver#query()` is documented to return `null` when the provider declines; old code called `c.getColumnNames()` directly → NPE → caught by broad `catch (Exception)` → opaque "Failed query" log with no rows. Added null guard; lets code fall through to publish an empty folder. |
| [`utils/CpuUtils.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/utils/CpuUtils.java) + [`batchops/BatchOpsService.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/batchops/BatchOpsService.java), [`profiles/ProfileApplierService.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/profiles/ProfileApplierService.java), [`apk/installer/PackageInstallerService.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/apk/installer/PackageInstallerService.java), [`logcat/LogcatRecordingService.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/logcat/LogcatRecordingService.java) | Systemic wake-lock leak | All 28 `WakeLock.acquire()` sites in the codebase used the no-timeout form; OS-kill between `acquire()` and `release()` leaks the lock until reboot (battery drain). Added `CpuUtils.acquireWakeLock(...)` helper with a 2-hour fallback timeout and routed the four foreground services through it. Remaining ~24 dialog/activity sites can be migrated incrementally. |
| [`rules/compontents/ComponentUtils.java`](app/src/main/java/io/github/muntashirakon/AppManager/rules/compontents/ComponentUtils.java) | IFW rules-import truncation | A single malformed `<component-filter name="…">` entry caused `ComponentName.unflattenFromString()` → null → NPE → caught by outer `catch (Throwable)` → **every subsequent rule in the file silently dropped**. Now skips just the bad entry; flipped `.equals()` direction for null-safety. |

### Iter-63 Out-of-Scope Follow-up (low priority)

- Migrate the remaining ~24 `wakeLock.acquire()` call sites in dialog/activity flows through `CpuUtils.acquireWakeLock` — mechanical sweep but each site needs to be eyeballed in case the caller deliberately wanted infinite hold.
- Remove the unreachable `AESCrypto.encrypt(InputStream, OutputStream)` / `decrypt(InputStream, OutputStream)` overloads — vestigial upstream code; no in-tree caller; would simplify the `Crypto` interface surface.
- `DiagnosticUtils.writeLogcat` does not drain `Process.getErrorStream()`; on modern Android the app can only read its own logcat so the pipe-fill deadlock is academic, but a clean fix is two lines.

---

## Premium Polish Track (v0.4.x → v0.7.x)

Parallel work-stream off the Onboarding theme (v0.4.0). The four-step rollout drafted in `design/plan/3-rollout.md` migrates AppManagerNG from the existing M3 token plane to a refined v2 token plane (calmer surfaces, tighter typography, pill-shaped FAB/search, outlined card variants). Each phase is independently revertable.

| Phase | Status | Scope |
|-------|--------|-------|
| ~~**v0.4.x Foundation**~~ ✅ shipped 2026-05-03 | Done | `app/src/main/res/values/{colors,dimens,themes}-v2.xml` copied verbatim from `design/impl/`. New pref `PREF_PREMIUM_PREVIEW_BOOL` (default OFF). `Prefs.Appearance.getAppTheme()` routes to `AppTheme.V2` / `AppTheme.V2.Amoled` when enabled, classic `AppTheme` / `AppTheme.Black` otherwise. Toggle exposed at Settings → Appearance → "Preview new design (BETA)". `getTransparentAppTheme()` deferred — transparent surfaces stay classic until v0.5.x. No layout files modified. |
| **v0.5.x Top-5 Surface Migration** — Phase 1 ✅ shipped 2026-05-02 | In Progress | Wired `activity_main_v2.xml` and `item_main_v2.xml` behind the toggle. MainActivity and MainRecyclerAdapter conditionally inflate v2 layouts. Phase 2: AppDetails / AppUsage / Settings surfaces. |
| **v0.6.x Default Flip** | Pending | Default `PREF_PREMIUM_PREVIEW_BOOL` to `true`; expose a "Use legacy design" escape hatch in Appearance for one release. |
| **v0.7.x Toggle Removal** | Pending | Delete the toggle, drop classic `AppTheme*` definitions, retire `colors-v2.xml`/`themes-v2.xml` filenames in favor of canonical `colors.xml`/`themes.xml`. |

---

## Rejected

| Item | Reason |
|------|--------|
| **Multi-device simultaneous ADB** (UAD-NG model) | UAD-NG is a desktop tool; AM/NG is on-device. This is a fundamentally different UX. WONTFIX. |
| **LSPatch integration** | LSPatch archived Dec 2023 (last release v0.6); no longer maintained; no viable path to integration ([S61]). WONTFIX. |
| **Play Store / APKMirror update tracking built-in** | Obtainium ([S26]) solves this with more sources and better maintenance. Out of scope; deep-link instead. |
| **Full on-device app store** | Aurora Store and F-Droid exist and are actively maintained. NG should complement, not replicate. |
| **App health score (single composite number)** | Collapses nuanced data into a single opinionated metric. AM's value is raw transparency; a score obscures it. Rejected — surface the component scores better instead. |
| **announceForAccessibility suppress-only fix** | Must do a real accessibility audit (T10), not suppress the deprecated API call without fixing the underlying UX. |
| **Backup of in-app purchase tokens / DRM state** | Not possible without root + OEM cooperation. Out of scope. |

---

## Upstream Sync Strategy

AppManagerNG is not a hard fork. The intent is to stay semantically close to upstream while diverging on UX.

**Pull policy:**
- Security fixes from upstream: pull immediately regardless of conflict cost.
- Bug fixes: cherry-pick within one upstream release cycle.
- Upstream "Upcoming Features" (Finder, APK editing, Routine Ops, Crash Monitor, Database Viewer, Terminal): pull when upstream ships rather than reimplement. NG reimplements only if upstream stalls for >12 months.

**Divergence tracking:**
- Weekly CI check comparing NG `main` against upstream `master`; generates cherry-pick candidate list.
- Maintained in `.github/upstream-sync.md` (to be created in v0.2.0).

**Current upstream "Upcoming Features" status:**

| Feature | Upstream Status | NG Action |
|---------|----------------|-----------|
| Finder | Partial code exists | Complete in NG (T7) |
| Basic APK editing | Committed, not shipped | Pull when ready (T12) |
| Routine operations | Spec published (Issue #61), not shipped | Implement in NG (T8) if stalled |
| Crash monitor | Mentioned only | Pull when ready |
| Database viewer/editor | Issue #14, not shipped | Pull when ready (T13) |
| Advanced terminal | Mentioned only | Pull when ready (T14) |
| Systemless ops | Issue #150, not shipped | Implement in NG (T15) |
| Import app list | Issue #122, not shipped | Implement in NG (T6) |
| Overlay management | Shipped v4.0.1 ([S39]) | Pull into T18 |
| app-manager:// deep link | Shipped v4.0.x ([S40]) | Pull into T18 |
| Operation history log | Shipped v4.0.0 ([S01]) | Implement in NG (T8) as medium-effort standalone feature — AM's implementation covers freeze, uninstall, backup; NG should match |
| Installer `package:` URI | Shipped v4.0.5 ([S01]) | Pull into T5 |
| Profile shortcut configured-state execution | Shipped v4.0.4 ([S01]) | Pull into T8 |
| v4.1.0 milestone (24 issues, 0 closed) | Due 2026-09-18; not yet started ([S40]) | Monitor; cherry-pick security/bug fixes when they land |
| v4.2.0 milestone (20+ issues confirmed open) | Issues #138, #150, #163, #221, #237, #256, #309, #321, #327, #333, #360, #385, #387, #402, #529, #568, #846, #1158, #1274, #1366, #1412, #1488 milestoned; none closed; upstream in-progress on #1017 | Implement #321 (Finder), #150 (Systemless), #568 (Backup extras), #163 (Crash monitor) in NG if upstream stalls past 12 months from milestone due date |
